function resizeCanvases() {\n            const canvases = document.querySelectorAll(\'.signature-canvas\');\n            canvases.forEach(canvas => {\n                const ratio = savedSignatures.client = clientSignaturePad.toDataURL();\n            }\n            localStorage.setItem(\'savedSignatures\', JSON.stringify(savedSignatures));\n showNotification(\'Progress saved successfully\', \'success\');\n        }\n        \n        function loadInitials() {\n            const savedInitials = localStorage.getItem(\'milestoneInitials\');\n            if (savedInitials) {\n                const initialsData = JSON.parse(savedInitials);\n                for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {\n (agencyInitials && initialsData[`stage${i}-agency`]) {\n                        agencyInitials.value = initialsData[`stage${i}-agency`];\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        function generatePDF() {\n            showNotification(\'Generating PDF...\', \'info\');\n            \n            // Hide buttons temporarily\n            const buttons = document.querySelectorAll(\'.signature-controls, .btn\');\n            buttons.forEach(btn => btn.style.display = \'none\');\n            \n imgData = canvas.toDataURL(\'image/png\');\n                const pdf = new jspdf.jsPDF(\'p\', \'mm\', \'a4\');\n                \n                const imgWidth = 210;\n                const pageHeight = 297;\n                const imgHeight = (canvas.height * imgWidth) / canvas.width;\n                let heightLeft = imgHeight;\n                let position = 0;\n                \n pageHeight;\n                }\n                \n                pdf.save(\'MMHH_Master_Services_Agreement.pdf\');\n                \n                // Show buttons again\n                buttons.forEach(btn => btn.style.display = btn.classList.contains(\'signature-controls\') ? \'flex\' : \'inline-block\');\n                \n                showNotification(\'PDF downloaded class="signature-pad-container">\n                    <label class="signature-label">AGENCY (MMHH)</label>\n                    <canvas id="agencySignature" class="signature-canvas"></canvas>\n                    <div class="signature-controls">\n                        <button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="clearSignature(\'agency\')">Clear</button>\n                        <button class="btn         <label class="signature-label">CLIENT (Curtis)</label>\n                    <canvas id="clientSignature" class="signature-canvas"></canvas>\n                    <div      \n        <div class="page-indicator">\n            PAGE 01 / 01\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    \n    <script>\n        let agencySignaturePad, clientSignaturePad;\n        let savedSignatures = {};\n        \n        // Initialize signature pads\n        function initializeSignatures() {\n            // Agency signature pad\n            const agencyCanvas = document.getElementById(\'agencySignature\');\n            agencySignaturePad = new SignaturePad(agencyCanvas, {\n                backgroundColor: \'rgba(0, 20, 40, 0.6)\',\n                penColor: \'#00ccff\',\n                minWidth: 1,\n                maxWidth: 3\n            });\n            \n            // Client signature pad\n            const clientCanvas = document.getElementById(\'clientSignature\');\n            clientSignaturePad = new SignaturePad(clientCanvas, {\n                backgroundColor: \'rgba(0, 20, 40, 0.6)\',\n                penColor: \'#00ccff\',\n                minWidth: 1,\n                maxWidth: 3\n            });\n            \n            // Load saved signatures if they exist\n            loadSavedSignatures();\n            loadInitials();\n            \n            // Set up canvas dimensions\n            resizeCanvases();\n            window.addEventListener(\'resize\', resizeCanvases);\n        }\n        \n        function resizeCanvases() {\n            const canvases = document.querySelectorAll(\'.signature-canvas\');\n            canvases.forEach(canvas => {\n                const ratio = Math.max(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 1);\n                canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth * ratio;\n                canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight * ratio;\n                canvas.getContext(\'2d\').scale(ratio, ratio);\n                \n                // Redraw signature if it exists\n                if (canvas.id === \'agencySignature\' && savedSignatures.agency) {\n                    agencySignaturePad.fromDataURL(savedSignatures.agency);\n                } else if (canvas.id === \'clientSignature\' && savedSignatures.client) {\n                    clientSignaturePad.fromDataURL(savedSignatures.client);\n                }\n            });\n        }\n        \n        function clearSignature(type) {\n            if (type === \'agency\') {\n                agencySignaturePad.clear();\n                delete savedSignatures.agency;\n            } else {\n                clientSignaturePad.clear();\n                delete savedSignatures.client;\n            }\n            localStorage.setItem(\'savedSignatures\', JSON.stringify(savedSignatures));\n            showNotification(\'Signature cleared\', \'info\');\n        }\n        \n        function saveSignature(type) {\n            if (type === \'agency\') {\n                if (agencySignaturePad.isEmpty()) {\n                    showNotification(\'Please provide a signature first\', \'error\');\n                    return;\n                }\n                savedSignatures.agency = agencySignaturePad.toDataURL();\n            } else {\n                if (clientSignaturePad.isEmpty()) {\n                    showNotification(\'Please provide a signature first\', \'error\');\n                    return;\n                }\n                savedSignatures.client = clientSignaturePad.toDataURL();\n            }\n            localStorage.setItem(\'savedSignatures\', JSON.stringify(savedSignatures));\n            showNotification(\'Signature saved successfully\', \'success\');\n        }\n        \n        function loadSavedSignatures() {\n            const saved = localStorage.getItem(\'savedSignatures\');\n            if (saved) {\n                savedSignatures = JSON.parse(saved);\n                \n                // Restore signatures\n                setTimeout(() => {\n                    if (savedSignatures.agency && agencySignaturePad) {\n                        agencySignaturePad.fromDataURL(savedSignatures.agency);\n                    }\n                    if (savedSignatures.client && clientSignaturePad) {\n                        clientSignaturePad.fromDataURL(savedSignatures.client);\n                    }\n                }, 100);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        function saveProgress() {\n            // Save signatures\n            localStorage.setItem(\'savedSignatures\', JSON.stringify(savedSignatures));\n            \n            // Save initials\n            const initialsData = {};\n            for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {\n                const clientInitials = document.getElementById(`stage${i}-initials`);\n                const agencyInitials = document.getElementById(`stage${i}-agency-initials`);\n                if (clientInitials) initialsData[`stage${i}-client`] = clientInitials.value;\n                if (agencyInitials) initialsData[`stage${i}-agency`] = agencyInitials.value;\n            }\n            localStorage.setItem(\'milestoneInitials\', JSON.stringify(initialsData));\n            \n            showNotification(\'Progress saved successfully\', \'success\');\n        }\n        \n        function loadInitials() {\n            const savedInitials = localStorage.getItem(\'milestoneInitials\');\n            if (savedInitials) {\n                const initialsData = JSON.parse(savedInitials);\n                for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {\n                    const clientInitials = document.getElementById(`stage${i}-initials`);\n                    const agencyInitials = document.getElementById(`stage${i}-agency-initials`);\n                    if (clientInitials && initialsData[`stage${i}-client`]) {\n                        clientInitials.value = initialsData[`stage${i}-client`];\n                    }\n                    if (agencyInitials && initialsData[`stage${i}-agency`]) {\n                        agencyInitials.value = initialsData[`stage${i}-agency`];\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        function generatePDF() {\n            showNotification(\'Generating PDF...\', \'info\');\n            \n            // Hide buttons temporarily\n            const buttons = document.querySelectorAll(\'.signature-controls, .btn\');\n            buttons.forEach(btn => btn.style.display = \'none\');\n            \n            html2canvas(document.querySelector(\'.container\'), {\n                scale: 2,\n                useCORS: true,\n                logging: false\n            }).then(canvas => {\n                const imgData = canvas.toDataURL(\'image/png\');\n                const pdf = new jspdf.jsPDF(\'p\', \'mm\', \'a4\');\n                \n                const imgWidth = 210;\n                const pageHeight = 297;\n                const imgHeight = (canvas.height * imgWidth) / canvas.width;\n                let heightLeft = imgHeight;\n                let position = 0;\n                \n                pdf.addImage(imgData, \'PNG\', 0, position, imgWidth, imgHeight);\n                heightLeft -= pageHeight;\n                \n                while (heightLeft >= 0) {\n                    position = heightLeft - imgHeight;\n                    pdf.addPage();\n                    pdf.addImage(imgData, \'PNG\', 0, position, imgWidth, imgHeight);\n                    heightLeft -= pageHeight;\n                }\n                \n                pdf.save(\'MMHH_Master_Services_Agreement.pdf\');\n                \n                // Show buttons again\n                buttons.forEach(btn => btn.style.display = btn.classList.contains(\'signature-controls\') ? \'flex\' : \'inline-block\');\n                \n                showNotification(\'PDF downloaded successfully\', \'success\');\n            }).catch(error => {\n                console.error(\'PDF generation error:\', error);\n                showNotification(\'Error generating PDF\', \'error\');\n                \n                // Show buttons again\n                buttons.forEach(btn => btn.style.display = btn.classList.contains(\'signature-controls\') ? \'flex\' : \'inline-block\');\n            });\n        }\n        \n        function showNotification(message, type) {\n            // Create notification element\n            const notification = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            notification.style.cssText = `\n                position: fixed;\n                top: 80px;\n                right: 20px;\n                padding: 15px 25px;\n                border-radius: 10px;\n                color: white;\n                font-weight: 600;\n                z-index: 10000;\n                font-family: \'Rajdhani\', sans-serif;\n                box-shadow: 0 5px 15px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);\n                max-width: 300px;\n            `;\n            \n            // Set background color based on type\n            if (type === \'success\') {\n                notification.style.background = \'linear-gradient(135deg, #00cc66, #00ff88)\';\n            } else if (type === \'error\') {\n                notification.style.background = \'linear-gradient(135deg, #ff4444, #ff6666)\';\n            } else {\n                notification.style.background = \'linear-gradient(135deg, #0066cc, #00ccff)\';\n            }\n            \n            notification.textContent = message;\n            document.body.appendChild(notification);\n            \n            // Animate in\n            notification.style.opacity = \'0\';\n            notification.style.transform = \'translateX(100%)\';\n            setTimeout(() => {\n                notification.style.transition = \'all 0.3s ease\';\n                notification.style.opacity = \'1\';\n                notification.style.transform = \'translateX(0)\';\n            }, 10);\n            \n            // Remove after 3 seconds\n            setTimeout(() => {\n                notification.style.opacity = \'0\';\n                notification.style.transform = \'translateX(100%)\';\n                setTimeout(() => {\n                    if (document.body.contains(notification)) {\n                        document.body.removeChild(notification);\n                    }\n                }, 300);\n            }, 3000);\n        }\n        \n        // Auto-save every 30 seconds\n        setInterval(saveProgress, 30000);\n        \n        // Initialize when page loads\n        document.addEventListener(\'DOMContentLoaded\', initializeSignatures);\n    </script>\n</body>\n</html>\n```\n\nThis is the complete, production-ready code for your Master Services Agreement website. buyerSignaturePad.fromDataURL(savedSignatures.buyer);\n                }\n            });\n        }\n        \n        function clearSignature(type) {\n            if (type === \'seller\') {\n                sellerSignaturePad.clear();\n                savedSignatures.seller = null;\n            } else {\n                buyerSignaturePad.clear();\n                savedSignatures.buyer = null;\n            }\n            localStorage.setItem(\'billOfSaleSignatures\', JSON.stringify(savedSignatures));\n            checkSignatures();\n            showNotification(\'Signature cleared\', localStorage.getItem(\'billOfSaleSignatures\');\n            if (saved) {\n                savedSignatures = JSON.parse(saved);\n                \n                // Restore signatures\n                  if (savedSignatures.buyer && buyerSignaturePad) {\n                        buyerSignaturePad.fromDataURL(savedSignatures.buyer);\n                    }\n savedSignatures.buyer;\n            const buttons = [\'downloadBtn\', \'printBtn\', \'emailBtn\'];\n            \n            buttons.forEach(btnId => {\n                const btn = document.getElementById(btnId);\n                if (bothSigned) {\n                    btn.classList.add(\'active\');\n                    btn.style.cursor = \'pointer\';\n                } else {\n                    btn.classList.remove(\'active\');\n                    btn.style.cursor = \'not-allowed\';\n                }\n            });\n        }\n        \n        function downloadPDF() {\n            if (!savedSignatures.seller || !savedSignatures.buyer) {\n                showNotification(\'Both signatures are required\', \'error\');\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            showNotification(\'Generating PDF...\', \'info\');\n            \n            // Hide buttons temporarily\n            const buttons =     }).then(canvas => {\n                const imgData = canvas.toDataURL(\'image/png\');\n                const pdf = new jspdf.jsPDF(\'p\', \'mm\', \'a4\');\n                \n                const imgWidth = 210;\n                const pageHeight = 297;\n                const imgHeight = (canvas.height * imgWidth) / canvas.width;\n                let heightLeft = imgHeight;\n                let position = 0;\n                \n                pdf.addImage(imgData, \'PNG\', 0, position, imgWidth, imgHeight);\n                heightLeft -= pageHeight;\n                \n                while (heightLeft >= 0) {\n                    position = heightLeft - imgHeight;\n                    pdf.addPage();\n                    pdf.addImage(imgData, \'PNG\', 0, position, imgWidth, imgHeight);\n                    heightLeft -= pageHeight;\n                }\n                \n                pdf.save(\'Bill_of_Sale_Method_Media.pdf\');\n                \n                // Show buttons again\n                buttons.forEach(btn => btn.style.display = btn.classList.contains(\'signature-controls\') ? \'flex\' : \'flex\');\n                \n                showNotification(\'PDF downloaded successfully\', \'success\');\n            }).catch(error => {\n                console.error(\'PDF generation error:\', error);\n                showNotification(\'Error generating PDF\', \'error\');\n                \n                // Show buttons again\n                buttons.forEach(btn => btn.style.display = btn.classList.contains(\'signature-controls\') ? \'flex\' : \'flex\');\n            });\n        }\n        \n        function emailDocument() {\n            if (!savedSignatures.seller || !savedSignatures.buyer) {\n                showNotification(\'Both showNotification(message, type) {\n            const notification = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            notification.style.cssText = `\n                position: fixed;\n                top: 80px;\n                right: 20px;\n                padding: 15px 25px;\n                border-radius: 10px;\n                color: white;\n                font-weight: 600;\n          if (type === \'success\') {\n                notification.style.background = \'linear-gradient(135deg, #00cc66, #00ff88)\';\n            } else if (type === \'error\') {\n                notification.style.background = \'linear-gradient(135deg, #ff4444, #ff6666)\';\n            } else {\n                notification.style.background = \'linear-gradient(135deg, #8a2be2, #ff1493)\';\n            }\n            \n            notification.textContent = message;\n            document.body.appendChild(notification);\n            \n            notification.style.opacity = \'0\';\n document.body.removeChild(notification);\n                    }\n                }, 300);\n            }, 3000);\n        }\n        \n        // Initialize when page loads\n
